    46	[37m;;; Commentary:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

    48	[37m;;; This file is the first thing loaded into Guile.  It adds many mundane[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    49	[37m;;; definitions and a few that are interesting.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

    57	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    58	[37m;;; {Deprecation}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    59	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    60	[37m[39;49;00m$
    61	[37m;; We don't have macros here, but we do want to define[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    62	[37m;; `begin-deprecated' early.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    63	[37m[39;49;00m$
    64	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mbegin-deprecated[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    65	[37m  [39;49;00m([32mprocedure->memoizing-macro[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    66	[37m   [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mexp[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31menv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    67	[37m     [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36minclude-deprecated-features[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    68	[37m	 [39;49;00m`([34mbegin[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m,@([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mexp[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
    69	[37m	 [39;49;00m`[31m#f[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
    70	[37m[39;49;00m$
    71	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    72	[37m;;; {Features}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    73	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    74	[37m[39;49;00m$
    75	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mprovide[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    76	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmemq[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m*features*[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
    77	[37m      [39;49;00m([34mset![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m*features*[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m*features*[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
    78	[37m[39;49;00m$
    79	[37m;;; Return #t iff FEATURE is available to this Guile interpreter.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    80	[37m;;; In SLIB, provided? also checks to see if the module is available.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    81	[37m;;; We should do that too, but don't.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    82	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mprovided?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfeature[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    83	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmemq[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfeature[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m*features*[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31m#t[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
    84	[37m[39;49;00m$
    85	([34mbegin-deprecated[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    86	[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mfeature?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    87	[37m   [39;49;00m([36missue-deprecation-warning[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    88	[37m    [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`feature?' is deprecated.  Use `provided?' instead.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    89	[37m   [39;49;00m([36mprovided?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
    90	[37m[39;49;00m$
    91	[37m;;; let format alias simple-format until the more complete version is loaded[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    92	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mformat[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36msimple-format[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    93	[37m[39;49;00m$
    94	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    95	[37m;;; {R4RS compliance}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    96	[37m[39;49;00m$
    97	([36mprimitive-load-path[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mice-9/r4rs.scm[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    98	[37m[39;49;00m$
    99	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   100	[37m;;; {Simple Debugging Tools}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   101	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   102	[37m[39;49;00m$
   103	[37m[39;49;00m$
   104	[37m;; peek takes any number of arguments, writes them to the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   105	[37m;; current ouput port, and returns the last argument.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   106	[37m;; It is handy to wrap around an expression to look at[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   107	[37m;; a value each time is evaluated, e.g.:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   108	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   109	[37m;;	(+ 10 (troublesome-fn))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   110	[37m;;	=> (+ 10 (pk 'troublesome-fn-returned (troublesome-fn)))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   111	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   112	[37m[39;49;00m$
   113	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mpeek[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   114	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mnewline[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   115	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m;;; [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   116	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mwrite[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   117	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mnewline[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   118	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlast-pair[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   119	[37m[39;49;00m$
   120	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mpk[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mpeek[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   121	[37m[39;49;00m$
   122	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mwarn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   123	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mwith-output-to-port[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcurrent-error-port[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   124	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m()[37m[39;49;00m$
   125	[37m      [39;49;00m([36mnewline[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   126	[37m      [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m;;; WARNING [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   127	[37m      [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   128	[37m      [39;49;00m([36mnewline[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   129	[37m      [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlast-pair[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   130	[37m[39;49;00m$
   131	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   132	[37m;;; {Trivial Functions}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   133	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   134	[37m[39;49;00m$
   135	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36midentity[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   136	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m1+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36m+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   137	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m1-[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36m+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m-1[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   138	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mand=>[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mprocedure[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mprocedure[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   139	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-hash-table[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mk[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-vector[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mk[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m'()))[37m[39;49;00m$
   140	[37m[39;49;00m$
   141	([34mbegin-deprecated[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   142	[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   143	[37m   [39;49;00m([36missue-deprecation-warning[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`id' is deprecated.  Use `identity' instead.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   144	[37m   [39;49;00m([36midentity[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   145	[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32m-1+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   146	[37m   [39;49;00m([36missue-deprecation-warning[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`-1+' is deprecated.  Use `1-' instead.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   147	[37m   [39;49;00m([36m1-[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   148	[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mreturn-it[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   149	[37m   [39;49;00m([36missue-deprecation-warning[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`return-it' is deprecated.  Use `noop' instead.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   150	[37m   [39;49;00m([36mapply[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mnoop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   151	[37m[39;49;00m$
   152	[37m;;; apply-to-args is functionally redundant with apply and, worse,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   153	[37m;;; is less general than apply since it only takes two arguments.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   154	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   155	[37m;;; On the other hand, apply-to-args is a syntacticly convenient way to[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   156	[37m;;; perform binding in many circumstances when the "let" family of[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   157	[37m;;; of forms don't cut it.  E.g.:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   158	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   159	[37m;;;	(apply-to-args (return-3d-mouse-coords)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   160	[37m;;;	  (lambda (x y z)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   161	[37m;;;		...))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   162	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   163	[37m[39;49;00m$
   164	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mapply-to-args[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfn[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mapply[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   165	[37m[39;49;00m$
   166	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   167	[37m[39;49;00m$
   168	[37m;;; {Integer Math}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   169	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   170	[37m[39;49;00m$
   171	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mipow-by-squaring[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mk[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31macc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

   271	[37m;; You can change that by giving a custom printing function to[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

   278	[37m[39;49;00m$

   419	[37m;;; {and-map and or-map}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   420	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   421	[37m;;; (and-map fn lst) is like (and (fn (car lst)) (fn (cadr lst)) (fn...) ...)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   422	[37m;;; (or-map fn lst) is like (or (fn (car lst)) (fn (cadr lst)) (fn...) ...)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   423	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   424	[37m[39;49;00m$
   425	[37m;; and-map f l[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   426	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   427	[37m;; Apply f to successive elements of l until exhaustion or f returns #f.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   428	[37m;; If returning early, return #f.  Otherwise, return the last value returned[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   429	[37m;; by f.  If f has never been called because l is empty, return #t.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   430	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   431	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mand-map[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mf[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mlst[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

   438	[37m[39;49;00m$

   646	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   647	[37m;;; {Help for scm_shell}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   648	[37m;;; The argument-processing code used by Guile-based shells generates[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   649	[37m;;; Scheme code based on the argument list.  This page contains help[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   650	[37m;;; functions for the code it generates.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   651	[37m[39;49;00m$
   652	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcommand-line[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mprogram-arguments[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   653	[37m[39;49;00m$
   654	[37m;; This is mostly for the internal use of the code generated by[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   655	[37m;; scm_compile_shell_switches.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   656	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mload-user-init[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   657	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet*[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mhome[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mgetenv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mHOME[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   658	[37m		   [39;49;00m([34mfalse-if-exception[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mpasswd:dir[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mgetpwuid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mgetuid[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   659	[37m		   [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m))[37m  [39;49;00m[37m;; fallback for cygwin etc.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   660	[37m	 [39;49;00m([32minit-file[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36min-vicinity[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mhome[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m.guile[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   661	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mfile-exists?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minit-file[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   662	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mprimitive-load[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minit-file[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   663	[37m[39;49;00m$
   664	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   665	[37m;;; {Loading by paths}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   666	[37m[39;49;00m$
   667	[37m;;; Load a Scheme source file named NAME, searching for it in the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   668	[37m;;; directories listed in %load-path, and applying each of the file[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   669	[37m;;; name extensions listed in %load-extensions.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   670	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mload-from-path[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   671	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mstart-stack[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'load-stack[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   672	[37m	       [39;49;00m([36mprimitive-load-path[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   673	[37m[39;49;00m$
   674	[37m[39;49;00m$
   675	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   676	[37m;;; {Transcendental Functions}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   677	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   678	[37m;;; Derived from "Transcen.scm", Complex trancendental functions for SCM.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   679	[37m;;; Written by Jerry D. Hedden, (C) FSF.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   680	[37m;;; See the file `COPYING' for terms applying to this program.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   681	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   682	[37m[39;49;00m$
   683	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mexp[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mz[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   684	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mreal?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mz[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([32m$exp[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mz[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   685	[37m      [39;49;00m([36mmake-polar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32m$exp[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mreal-part[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mz[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m([36mimag-part[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mz[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   686	[37m[39;49;00m$
   687	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlog[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mz[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   688	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mreal?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mz[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36m>=[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mz[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m0[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   689	[37m      [39;49;00m([32m$log[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mz[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

   898	[37m	 [39;49;00m([32mtransmogrified-cases[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmap[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mcase[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   899	[37m				      [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mopts[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mcase[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   900	[37m					      [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mboolean?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopts[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36meq?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'else[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopts[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   901	[37m						  [39;49;00m[31mopts[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

   904	[37m						   [39;49;00m(([36mboolean?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopts[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m[31mopts[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   905	[37m						   [39;49;00m(([36mstring?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcaar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopts[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopts[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   906	[37m						   [39;49;00m([34melse[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopts[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   907	[37m					    [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mcase[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   908	[37m				    [39;49;00m[31mcases[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   909	[37m    [39;49;00m`([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32m%display-usage[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m()[37m [39;49;00m([32mdisplay-usage-report[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m',usage-desc[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   910	[37m       [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32m%argv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   911	[37m	 [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%next-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32m%argv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%argv[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   912	[37m	   [39;49;00m([32mget-option[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%argv[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   913	[37m		       [39;49;00m[33m',kw-opts[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   914	[37m		       [39;49;00m[33m',kw-args[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   915	[37m		       [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32m%opt[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%new-argv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   916	[37m			 [39;49;00m([34mcase[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%opt[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   917	[37m			   [39;49;00m,@[37m [39;49;00m[31mtransmogrified-cases[39;49;00m))))))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   918	[37m[39;49;00m$
   919	[37m[39;49;00m$
   920	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   921	[37m[39;49;00m$
   922	[37m;;; {Low Level Modules}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   923	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   924	[37m;;; These are the low level data structures for modules.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   925	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   926	[37m;;; !!! warning: The interface to lazy binder procedures is going[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   927	[37m;;; to be changed in an incompatible way to permit all the basic[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   928	[37m;;; module ops to be virtualized.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   929	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   930	[37m;;; (make-module size use-list lazy-binding-proc) => module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   931	[37m;;; module-{obarray,uses,binder}[|-set!][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   932	[37m;;; (module? obj) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   933	[37m;;; (module-locally-bound? module symbol) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   934	[37m;;; (module-bound? module symbol) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   935	[37m;;; (module-symbol-locally-interned? module symbol) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   936	[37m;;; (module-symbol-interned? module symbol) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   937	[37m;;; (module-local-variable module symbol) => [#<variable ...> | #f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   938	[37m;;; (module-variable module symbol) => [#<variable ...> | #f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   939	[37m;;; (module-symbol-binding module symbol opt-value)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   940	[37m;;;		=> [ <obj> | opt-value | an error occurs ][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   941	[37m;;; (module-make-local-var! module symbol) => #<variable...>[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   942	[37m;;; (module-add! module symbol var) => unspecified[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   943	[37m;;; (module-remove! module symbol) =>  unspecified[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   944	[37m;;; (module-for-each proc module) => unspecified[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   945	[37m;;; (make-scm-module) => module ; a lazy copy of the symhash module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   946	[37m;;; (set-current-module module) => unspecified[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   947	[37m;;; (current-module) => #<module...>[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   948	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   949	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   950	[37m[39;49;00m$
   951	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   952	[37m;;; {Printing Modules}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   953	[37m;; This is how modules are printed.  You can re-define it.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   954	[37m;; (Redefining is actually more complicated than simply redefining[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   955	[37m;; %print-module because that would only change the binding and not[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   956	[37m;; the value stored in the vtable that determines how record are[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   957	[37m;; printed. Sigh.)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   958	[37m[39;49;00m$
   959	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m%print-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m  [39;49;00m[37m; unused args: depth length style table)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   960	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m#<[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   961	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-kind[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mmodule[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   962	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-name[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   963	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   964	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mbegin[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   965	[37m	  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   966	[37m	  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   967	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   968	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnumber->string[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mobject-address[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[34m16[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   969	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m>[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   970	[37m[39;49;00m$
   971	[37m;; module-type[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   972	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   973	[37m;; A module is characterized by an obarray in which local symbols[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   974	[37m;; are interned, a list of modules, "uses", from which non-local[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   975	[37m;; bindings can be inherited, and an optional lazy-binder which[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   976	[37m;; is a (CLOSURE module symbol) which, as a last resort, can provide[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   977	[37m;; bindings that would otherwise not be found locally in the module.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   978	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   979	[37m;; NOTE: If you change here, you also need to change libguile/modules.h.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   980	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   981	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   982	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmake-record-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   983	[37m		    [39;49;00m'([31mobarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31muses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31meval-closure[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mtransformer[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkind[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   984	[37m			      [39;49;00m[31mobservers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mweak-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mobserver-id[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   985	[37m		    [39;49;00m[36m%print-module[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   986	[37m[39;49;00m$
   987	[37m;; make-module &opt size uses binder[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   988	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   989	[37m;; Create a new module, perhaps with a particular size of obarray,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   990	[37m;; initial uses list, or binding procedure.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   991	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   992	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmake-module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   993	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   994	[37m[39;49;00m$
   995	[37m      [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mparse-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mindex[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mdefault[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   996	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m>[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlength[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mindex[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   997	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36mlist-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mindex[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   998	[37m	    [39;49;00m[31mdefault[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   999	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1000	[37m      [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m>[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlength[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[34m3[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1001	[37m	  [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mToo many args to make-module.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1002	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1003	[37m      [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32msize[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mparse-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m0[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1021[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1004	[37m	    [39;49;00m([32muses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mparse-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m'()))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1005	[37m	    [39;49;00m([32mbinder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mparse-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m2[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1006	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1007	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36minteger?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msize[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1008	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mIllegal size to make-module.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msize[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1009	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlist?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31muses[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1011	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mIncorrect use list.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31muses[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1012	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mprocedure?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1013	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1014	[37m	     [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mLazy-binder expected to be a procedure or #f.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1015	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1016	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-constructor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-vector[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msize[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m'())[37m[39;49;00m$
  1017	[37m					  [39;49;00m[31muses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1018	[37m					  [39;49;00m'()[37m[39;49;00m$
  1019	[37m					  [39;49;00m([36mmake-weak-value-hash-table[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m31[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1020	[37m					  [39;49;00m[34m0[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1021	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1022	[37m	  [39;49;00m[37m;; We can't pass this as an argument to module-constructor,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1023	[37m	  [39;49;00m[37m;; because we need it to close over a pointer to the module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1024	[37m	  [39;49;00m[37m;; itself.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1025	[37m	  [39;49;00m([32mset-module-eval-closure![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mstandard-eval-closure[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$

  1028	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1029	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-constructor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mrecord-constructor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1030	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m  [39;49;00m([36mrecord-accessor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'obarray[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$

  1047	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mset-module-observers![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mrecord-modifier[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'observers[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1048	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-weak-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mrecord-accessor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'weak-observers[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1049	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-observer-id[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mrecord-accessor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'observer-id[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1050	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mset-module-observer-id![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mrecord-modifier[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'observer-id[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1051	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mrecord-predicate[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1052	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1053	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mset-module-eval-closure![39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1054	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([36msetter[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mrecord-modifier[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'eval-closure[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1055	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mclosure[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1056	[37m      [39;49;00m([36msetter[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mclosure[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1057	[37m      [39;49;00m[37m;; Make it possible to lookup the module from the environment.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1058	[37m      [39;49;00m[37m;; This implementation is correct since an eval closure can belong[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1059	[37m      [39;49;00m[37m;; to maximally one module.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1060	[37m      [39;49;00m([36mset-procedure-property![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mclosure[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1061	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1062	([34mbegin-deprecated[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1063	[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32meval-in-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mexp[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1064	[37m   [39;49;00m([36missue-deprecation-warning[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1065	[37m    [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`eval-in-module' is deprecated.  Use `eval' instead.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1066	[37m   [39;49;00m([36meval[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mexp[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1067	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1068	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1069	[37m;;; {Observer protocol}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1070	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1071	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1072	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-observe[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1073	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mset-module-observers![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1074	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1075	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1076	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-observe-weak[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1077	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mmodule-observer-id[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1078	[37m    [39;49;00m([36mhash-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-weak-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1079	[37m    [39;49;00m([32mset-module-observer-id![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1080	[37m    [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1081	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1082	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-unobserve[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mtoken[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1083	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mtoken[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1084	[37m	[39;49;00m([32mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mtoken[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1085	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36minteger?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1086	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mhash-remove![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-weak-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1087	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mset-module-observers![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mdelq1![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1088	[37m  [39;49;00m[34m*unspecified*[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1089	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1090	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-modified[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1091	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mfor-each[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mproc[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([32mproc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1092	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mhash-fold[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mres[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([32mproc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-weak-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1093	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1094	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1095	[37m;;; {Module Searching in General}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1096	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1097	[37m;;; We sometimes want to look for properties of a symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1098	[37m;;; just within the obarray of one module.  If the property[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1099	[37m;;; holds, then it is said to hold ``locally'' as in, ``The symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1100	[37m;;; DISPLAY is locally rebound in the module `safe-guile'.''[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1101	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1102	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1103	[37m;;; Other times, we want to test for a symbol property in the obarray[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1104	[37m;;; of M and, if it is not found there, try each of the modules in the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1105	[37m;;; uses list of M.  This is the normal way of testing for some[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1106	[37m;;; property, so we state these properties without qualification as[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1107	[37m;;; in: ``The symbol 'fnord is interned in module M because it is[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1108	[37m;;; interned locally in module M2 which is a member of the uses list[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1109	[37m;;; of M.''[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1110	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1111	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1112	[37m;; module-search fn m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1113	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1114	[37m;; return the first non-#f result of FN applied to M and then to[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1115	[37m;; the modules in the uses of m, and so on recursively.  If all applications[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1116	[37m;; return #f, then so does this function.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1117	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1118	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1119	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mpos[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1120	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mpair?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mpos[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1121	[37m	 [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mpos[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1122	[37m	     [39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mpos[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1123	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mfn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1124	[37m      [39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-uses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1125	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1126	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1127	[37m;;; {Is a symbol bound in a module?}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1128	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1129	[37m;;; Symbol S in Module M is bound if S is interned in M and if the binding[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1130	[37m;;; of S in M has been set to some well-defined value.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1131	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1132	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1133	[37m;; module-locally-bound? module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1134	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1135	[37m;; Is a symbol bound (interned and defined) locally in a given module?[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1136	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1137	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-locally-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1138	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1139	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1140	[37m	 [39;49;00m([36mvariable-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1141	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1142	[37m;; module-bound? module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1143	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1144	[37m;; Is a symbol bound (interned and defined) anywhere in a given module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1145	[37m;; or its uses?[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1146	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1147	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1148	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-locally-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1149	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1150	[37m;;; {Is a symbol interned in a module?}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1151	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1152	[37m;;; Symbol S in Module M is interned if S occurs in[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1153	[37m;;; of S in M has been set to some well-defined value.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1154	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1155	[37m;;; It is possible to intern a symbol in a module without providing[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1156	[37m;;; an initial binding for the corresponding variable.  This is done[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1157	[37m;;; with:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1158	[37m;;;       (module-add! module symbol (make-undefined-variable))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1159	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1160	[37m;;; In that case, the symbol is interned in the module, but not[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1161	[37m;;; bound there.  The unbound symbol shadows any binding for that[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1162	[37m;;; symbol that might otherwise be inherited from a member of the uses list.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1163	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1164	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1165	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-get-handle[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1166	[37m  [39;49;00m(([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36msymbol?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[36mhashq-get-handle[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mhash-get-handle[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1167	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1168	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1169	[37m  [39;49;00m(([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36msymbol?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[36mhashq-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mhash-ref[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1170	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1171	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1172	[37m  [39;49;00m(([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36msymbol?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[36mhashq-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mhash-set![39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1173	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1174	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-remove![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1175	[37m  [39;49;00m(([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36msymbol?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[36mhashq-remove![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mhash-remove![39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1176	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1177	[37m;; module-symbol-locally-interned? module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1178	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1179	[37m;; is a symbol interned (not neccessarily defined) locally in a given module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1180	[37m;; or its uses?  Interned symbols shadow inherited bindings even if[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1181	[37m;; they are not themselves bound to a defined value.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1182	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1183	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-symbol-locally-interned?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1184	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-get-handle[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1185	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1186	[37m;; module-symbol-interned? module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1187	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1188	[37m;; is a symbol interned (not neccessarily defined) anywhere in a given module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1189	[37m;; or its uses?  Interned symbols shadow inherited bindings even if[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1190	[37m;; they are not themselves bound to a defined value.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1191	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1192	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-symbol-interned?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1193	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-symbol-locally-interned?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1194	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1195	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1196	[37m;;; {Mapping modules x symbols --> variables}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1197	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1198	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1199	[37m;; module-local-variable module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1200	[37m;; return the local variable associated with a MODULE and SYMBOL.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1201	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1202	[37m;;; This function is very important. It is the only function that can[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1203	[37m;;; return a variable from a module other than the mutators that store[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1204	[37m;;; new variables in modules.  Therefore, this function is the location[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1205	[37m;;; of the "lazy binder" hack.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1206	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1207	[37m;;; If symbol is defined in MODULE, and if the definition binds symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1208	[37m;;; to a variable, return that variable object.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1209	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1210	[37m;;; If the symbols is not found at first, but the module has a lazy binder,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1211	[37m;;; then try the binder.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1212	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1213	[37m;;; If the symbol is not found at all, return #f.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1214	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1215	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1216	[37m;  (caddr[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1217	[37m;   (list m v[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1218	[37m	 [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mb[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1219	[37m	   [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mvariable?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mb[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mb[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1220	[37m	       [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-binder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1221	[37m		    [39;49;00m(([36mmodule-binder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1222	[37m;))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1223	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1224	[37m;; module-variable module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1225	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1226	[37m;; like module-local-variable, except search the uses in the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1227	[37m;; case V is not found in M.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1228	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1229	[37m;; NOTE: This function is superseded with C code (see modules.c)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1230	[37m;;;      when using the standard eval closure.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1231	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1232	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1233	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1234	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1235	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1236	[37m;;; {Mapping modules x symbols --> bindings}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1237	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1238	[37m;;; These are similar to the mapping to variables, except that the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1239	[37m;;; variable is dereferenced.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1240	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1241	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1242	[37m;; module-symbol-binding module symbol opt-value[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1243	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1244	[37m;; return the binding of a variable specified by name within[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1245	[37m;; a given module, signalling an error if the variable is unbound.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1246	[37m;; If the OPT-VALUE is passed, then instead of signalling an error,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1247	[37m;; return OPT-VALUE.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1248	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1249	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-symbol-local-binding[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1250	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1251	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1252	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mvariable-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1253	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1254	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1255	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mLocally unbound variable.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1256	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1257	[37m;; module-symbol-binding module symbol opt-value[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1258	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1259	[37m;; return the binding of a variable specified by name within[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1260	[37m;; a given module, signalling an error if the variable is unbound.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1261	[37m;; If the OPT-VALUE is passed, then instead of signalling an error,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1262	[37m;; return OPT-VALUE.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1263	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1264	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-symbol-binding[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1265	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1266	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1267	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mvariable-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1268	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1269	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1270	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mUnbound variable.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1271	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1272	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1273	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1274	[37m;;; {Adding Variables to Modules}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1275	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1276	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1277	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1278	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1279	[37m;; module-make-local-var! module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1280	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1281	[37m;; ensure a variable for V in the local namespace of M.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1282	[37m;; If no variable was already there, then create a new and uninitialzied[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1283	[37m;; variable.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1284	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1285	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-make-local-var![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1286	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mb[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1287	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mvariable?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mb[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1288	[37m	     [39;49;00m([34mbegin[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1289	[37m	       [39;49;00m([36mmodule-modified[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1290	[37m	       [39;49;00m[31mb[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1291	[37m      [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-binder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1292	[37m	   [39;49;00m(([36mmodule-binder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#t[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1293	[37m      [39;49;00m([34mbegin[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1294	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32manswer[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-undefined-variable[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1295	[37m	  [39;49;00m([32mvariable-set-name-hint![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31manswer[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1296	[37m	  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31manswer[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1297	[37m	  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-modified[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1298	[37m	  [39;49;00m[31manswer[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1299	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1300	[37m;; module-ensure-local-variable! module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1301	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1302	[37m;; Ensure that there is a local variable in MODULE for SYMBOL.  If[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1303	[37m;; there is no binding for SYMBOL, create a new uninitialized[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1304	[37m;; variable.  Return the local variable.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1305	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1306	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-ensure-local-variable![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36msymbol[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1307	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36msymbol[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1308	[37m      [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-undefined-variable[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1309	[37m	[39;49;00m([32mvariable-set-name-hint![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36msymbol[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1310	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mmodule-add![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36msymbol[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1311	[37m	[39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1312	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1313	[37m;; module-add! module symbol var[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1314	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1315	[37m;; ensure a particular variable for V in the local namespace of M.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1316	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1369	[37m;; make-root-module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1428	[37m;;; {MODULE-REF -- exported}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1429	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1430	[37m;; Returns the value of a variable called NAME in MODULE or any of its[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1436	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mvariable-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1437	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mvariable-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1439	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mNo variable named[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'in[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1440	[37m	    [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mrest[39;49;00m)[37m			[39;49;00m[37m; default value[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1441	[37m	    [39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1442	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1443	[37m;; MODULE-SET! -- exported[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1444	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1445	[37m;; Sets the variable called NAME in MODULE (or in a module that MODULE uses)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1446	[37m;; to VALUE; if there is no such variable, an error is signaled.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1447	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1448	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1449	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1450	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1451	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mvariable-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1452	[37m	[39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mNo variable named[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'in[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1453	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1454	[37m;; MODULE-DEFINE! -- exported[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1455	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1456	[37m;; Sets the variable called NAME in MODULE to VALUE; if there is no such[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1457	[37m;; variable, it is added first.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1458	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1459	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-define![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1460	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1461	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1462	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mbegin[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1463	[37m	  [39;49;00m([36mvariable-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1464	[37m	  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-modified[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1465	[37m	[39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1466	[37m	  [39;49;00m([32mvariable-set-name-hint![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1467	[37m	  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-add![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1468	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1469	[37m;; MODULE-DEFINED? -- exported[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1470	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1471	[37m;; Return #t iff NAME is defined in MODULE (or in a module that MODULE[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1472	[37m;; uses)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1473	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1474	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-defined?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1475	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1476	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mvariable-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1477	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1478	[37m;; MODULE-USE! module interface[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1479	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1480	[37m;; Add INTERFACE to the list of interfaces used by MODULE.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1481	[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1482	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-use![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minterface[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1483	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mset-module-uses![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1484	[37m		    [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minterface[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mdelq![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minterface[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-uses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1485	[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-modified[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1486	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1487	[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1488	[37m;;; {Recursive Namespaces}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1489	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1490	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1491	[37m;;; A hierarchical namespace emerges if we consider some module to be[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1492	[37m;;; root, and variables bound to modules as nested namespaces.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1493	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1494	[37m;;; The routines in this file manage variable names in hierarchical namespace.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1495	[37m;;; Each variable name is a list of elements, looked up in successively nested[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1496	[37m;;; modules.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1497	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1498	[37m;;;		(nested-ref some-root-module '(foo bar baz))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1499	[37m;;;		=> <value of a variable named baz in the module bound to bar in[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1500	[37m;;;		    the module bound to foo in some-root-module>[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1501	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1502	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1503	[37m;;; There are:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1504	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1505	[37m;;;	;; a-root is a module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1506	[37m;;;	;; name is a list of symbols[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1507	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1508	[37m;;;	nested-ref a-root name[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1509	[37m;;;	nested-set! a-root name val[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1510	[37m;;;	nested-define! a-root name val[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1511	[37m;;;	nested-remove! a-root name[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1512	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1513	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1514	[37m;;; (current-module) is a natural choice for a-root so for convenience there are[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1515	[37m;;; also:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1516	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1517	[37m;;;	local-ref name		==	nested-ref (current-module) name[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1518	[37m;;;	local-set! name val	==	nested-set! (current-module) name val[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1519	[37m;;;	local-define! name val	==	nested-define! (current-module) name val[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1520	[37m;;;	local-remove! name	==	nested-remove! (current-module) name[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1521	[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1522	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1523	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1524	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1525	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1526	[37m	     [39;49;00m([32melts[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1527	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mcond[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1528	[37m     [39;49;00m(([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m)[37m		[39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1529	[37m     [39;49;00m(([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m))[37m	[39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1530	[37m     [39;49;00m([34melse[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m))))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1531	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1532	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1533	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1534	[37m	     [39;49;00m([32melts[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1535	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1536	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mmodule-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1537	[37m	[39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1538	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1539	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-define![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1540	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1541	[37m	     [39;49;00m([32melts[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1542	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1543	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mmodule-define![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1544	[37m	[39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1545	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1546	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-remove![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1547	[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1548	[37m	     [39;49;00m([32melts[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1549	[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1550	[37m	[39;49;00m([36mmodule-remove![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1551	[37m	[39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1552	[37m[39;49;00m$
  1553	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlocal-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcurrent-module[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1554	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlocal-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcurrent-module[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1555	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlocal-define[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-define![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcurrent-module[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1556	([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlocal-remove[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-remove![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcurrent-module[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
